    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [t].[IdRol] = [r].[Id]

SELECT [r].[Id], [r].[Nombre]
FROM [Roles] AS [r]
